DCU HW       DCU Hardware (DCU Streamer) fetches the next cache line into the L1 cache.                                                                                   0x01A4   2     Enabled

DCU NP       DCU Next Page is an L1 data cache prefetcher.                                                                                                                0x01A4   4     Enabled
AMP          Adaptive Multipath Probability (MLC AMP) predicts access patterns based on previous patterns and fetches the corresponding cache lines into the L2 cache.    0x01A4   5     Enabled
